***advocatuur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:advocatuur.html>advocatuur</a> (41150)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Advokatur</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:advocaat.html>advocaat</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-uur</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:advocatuur.html>advocatuur</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:advocatuur.html>advocaturen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lawyer.html>lawyer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:profession.html>profession</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
